  x eslint(complexity): function `dereferenceNode` has a complexity of 15. Maximum allowed is 12.
    ,-[packages/ai/src/utils/schema/dereference.ts:34:1]
 33 |      */
 34 | ,-> function dereferenceNode(node: unknown, root: JsonObject, visiting: Set<string>): unknown {
 35 | |       if (!isJsonObject(node)) return node;
 36 | |       if (Array.isArray(node)) return node.map(item => dereferenceNode(item, root, visiting));
 37 | |   
 38 | |       const ref = node.$ref;
 39 | |       if (typeof ref === "string") {
 40 | |           // Break circular references
 41 | |           if (visiting.has(ref)) return {};
 42 | |           const resolved = resolveLocalRef(ref, root);
 43 | |           if (!resolved) return node; // External ref — leave as-is
 44 | |           visiting.add(ref);
 45 | |           const inlined = dereferenceNode(resolved, root, visiting);
 46 | |           visiting.delete(ref);
 47 | |   
 48 | |           // Merge sibling keywords (e.g. description, default) from the
 49 | |           // referencing node. In draft 2020-12 these are valid alongside $ref.
 50 | |           const hasSiblings = Object.keys(node).some(k => k !== "$ref");
 51 | |           if (!hasSiblings || !isJsonObject(inlined)) return inlined;
 52 | |           const merged: JsonObject = { ...inlined };
 53 | |           for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(node)) {
 54 | |               if (key !== "$ref") merged[key] = value;
 55 | |           }
 56 | |           return merged;
 57 | |       }
 58 | |   
 59 | |       const result: JsonObject = {};
 60 | |       for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(node)) {
 61 | |           // Skip $defs/definitions — they get inlined into consumers
 62 | |           if (key === "$defs" || key === "definitions") continue;
 63 | |   
 64 | |           if (Array.isArray(value)) {
 65 | |               result[key] = value.map(item => dereferenceNode(item, root, visiting));
 66 | |           } else if (isJsonObject(value)) {
 67 | |               result[key] = dereferenceNode(value, root, visiting);
 68 | |           } else {
 69 | |               result[key] = value;
 70 | |           }
 71 | |       }
 72 | |       return result;

  ! eslint(max-lines-per-function): The function `transformMessages` has too many lines (223). Maximum allowed is 50.
     ,-[packages/ai/src/providers/transform-messages.ts:21:8]

  21 | ,-> export function transformMessages<TApi extends Api>(
  22 | |       messages: Message[],
  23 | |       model: Model<TApi>,
  24 | |       normalizeToolCallId?: (id: string, model: Model<TApi>, source: AssistantMessage) => string,
  25 | |   ): Message[] {
  26 | |       // Build a map of original tool call IDs to normalized IDs
  27 | |       const toolCallIdMap = new Map<string, string>();
  28 | |   
  29 | |       const latestAssistantIndex = messages.findLastIndex(msg => msg.role === "assistant");
  30 | |       // First pass: transform messages (thinking blocks, tool call ID normalization)
  31 | |       const transformed = messages.map((msg, index) => {
  32 | |           // User and developer messages pass through unchanged
  33 | |           if (msg.role === "user" || msg.role === "developer") {
  34 | |               return msg;
  35 | |           }
  36 | |   
  37 | |           // Handle toolResult messages - normalize toolCallId if we have a mapping
  38 | |           if (msg.role === "toolResult") {
  39 | |               const normalizedId = toolCallIdMap.get(msg.toolCallId);
  40 | |               if (
  41 | |                   normalizedId !== null &&
  42 | |                   normalizedId !== undefined &&
  43 | |                   normalizedId !== "" &&
  44 | |                   normalizedId !== msg.toolCallId
  45 | |               ) {
  46 | |                   return { ...msg, toolCallId: normalizedId };
  47 | |               }
  48 | |               return msg;
  49 | |           }
  50 | |   
  51 | |           // Assistant messages need transformation check
  52 | |           if (msg.role === "assistant") {
  53 | |               const assistantMsg = msg as AssistantMessage;
  54 | |               const isSameModel =
  55 | |                   assistantMsg.provider === model.provider &&
  56 | |                   assistantMsg.api === model.api &&
  57 | |                   assistantMsg.model === model.id;
  58 | |   
  59 | |               const mustPreserveLatestAnthropicThinking =
  60 | |                   index === latestAssistantIndex &&
  61 | |                   model.api === "anthropic-messages" &&
  62 | |                   assistantMsg.api === "anthropic-messages";
  63 | |               // Aborted/errored messages may have partially-streamed thinking signatures.
  64 | |               // A partial signature is invalid and will be rejected by the API, so we must
  65 | |               // strip signatures from thinking blocks in these messages.
  66 | |               const hasInvalidSignatures = assistantMsg.stopReason === "aborted" || assistantMsg.stopReason === "error";
  67 | |   
  68 | |               const transformedContent = assistantMsg.content.flatMap(block => {
  69 | |                   if (block.type === "thinking") {
  70 | |                       // Strip signature from aborted/errored messages — it's likely incomplete
  71 | |                       const sanitized =
  72 | |                           hasInvalidSignatures &&
  73 | |                           block.thinkingSignature !== null &&
  74 | |                           block.thinkingSignature !== undefined &&
  75 | |                           block.thinkingSignature !== ""
  76 | |                               ? { ...block, thinkingSignature: undefined }
  77 | |                               : block;
  78 | |                       if (mustPreserveLatestAnthropicThinking) return sanitized;
  79 | |                       // For same model: keep thinking blocks with signatures (needed for replay)
  80 | |                       // even if the thinking text is empty (OpenAI encrypted reasoning)
  81 | |                       if (
  82 | |                           isSameModel &&
  83 | |                           sanitized.thinkingSignature !== null &&
  84 | |                           sanitized.thinkingSignature !== undefined &&
  85 | |                           sanitized.thinkingSignature !== ""
  86 | |                       )
  87 | |                           return sanitized;
  88 | |                       // Skip empty thinking blocks, convert others to plain text
  89 | |                       if (!sanitized.thinking || sanitized.thinking.trim() === "") return [];
  90 | |                       if (isSameModel) return sanitized;
  91 | |                       return {
  92 | |                           type: "text" as const,
  93 | |                           text: sanitized.thinking,
  94 | |                       };
  95 | |                   }
  96 | |   
  97 | |                   if (block.type === "redactedThinking") {
  98 | |                       if (mustPreserveLatestAnthropicThinking) return block;
  99 | |                       if (isSameModel) return block;
 100 | |                       return [];
 101 | |                   }
 102 | |   
 103 | |                   if (block.type === "text") {
 104 | |                       if (isSameModel) return block;
 105 | |                       return {
 106 | |                           type: "text" as const,
 107 | |                           text: block.text,
 108 | |                       };
 109 | |                   }
 110 | |   
 111 | |                   if (block.type === "toolCall") {
 112 | |                       const toolCall = block as ToolCall;
 113 | |                       let normalizedToolCall: ToolCall = toolCall;
 114 | |   
 115 | |                       if (
 116 | |                           !isSameModel &&
 117 | |                           toolCall.thoughtSignature !== null &&
 118 | |                           toolCall.thoughtSignature !== undefined &&
 119 | |                           toolCall.thoughtSignature !== ""
 120 | |                       ) {
 121 | |                           normalizedToolCall = { ...toolCall };
 122 | |                           delete (normalizedToolCall as { thoughtSignature?: string }).thoughtSignature;
 123 | |                       }
 124 | |   
 125 | |                       if (!isSameModel && normalizeToolCallId) {
 126 | |                           const normalizedId = normalizeToolCallId(toolCall.id, model, assistantMsg);
 127 | |                           if (normalizedId !== toolCall.id) {
 128 | |                               toolCallIdMap.set(toolCall.id, normalizedId);
 129 | |                               normalizedToolCall = { ...normalizedToolCall, id: normalizedId };
 130 | |                           }
 131 | |                       }
 132 | |   
 133 | |                       return normalizedToolCall;
 134 | |                   }
 135 | |   
 136 | |                   return block;
 137 | |               });
 138 | |   
 139 | |               return {
 140 | |                   ...assistantMsg,
 141 | |                   content: transformedContent,
 142 | |               };
 143 | |           }
 144 | |           return msg;
 145 | |       });
 146 | |       const realToolResultIds = new Set(
 147 | |           transformed.filter((msg): msg is ToolResultMessage => msg.role === "toolResult").map(msg => msg.toolCallId),
 148 | |       );
 149 | |   
 150 | |       // Second pass: insert synthetic empty tool results for orphaned tool calls
 151 | |       // and preserve aborted/errored tool results when they were already persisted.
 152 | |       const result: Message[] = [];
 153 | |       let pendingToolCalls: ToolCall[] = [];
 154 | |       let pendingAbortedToolCalls = new Map<string, ToolCall>();
 155 | |       let pendingAbortedTimestamp: number | undefined;
 156 | |       // Track tool call status: whether resolved (has result) or aborted (synthetic result injected, skip later real results)
 157 | |       const toolCallStatus = new Map<string, ToolCallStatus>();
 158 | |   
 159 | |       const flushPendingToolCalls = (timestamp: number): void => {
 160 | |           if (pendingToolCalls.length === 0) return;
 161 | |           for (const tc of pendingToolCalls) {
 162 | |               if (!toolCallStatus.has(tc.id) && !realToolResultIds.has(tc.id)) {
 163 | |                   result.push({
 164 | |                       role: "toolResult",
 165 | |                       toolCallId: tc.id,
 166 | |                       toolName: tc.name,
 167 | |                       content: [{ type: "text", text: "No result provided" }],
 168 | |                       isError: true,
 169 | |                       timestamp,
 170 | |                   } as ToolResultMessage);
 171 | |                   toolCallStatus.set(tc.id, ToolCallStatus.Resolved);
 172 | |               }
 173 | |           }
 174 | |           pendingToolCalls = [];
 175 | |       };
 176 | |   
 177 | |       const flushPendingAbortedToolCalls = (): void => {
 178 | |           if (pendingAbortedTimestamp === undefined) return;
 179 | |           for (const tc of pendingAbortedToolCalls.values()) {
 180 | |               if (!toolCallStatus.has(tc.id)) {
 181 | |                   result.push({
 182 | |                       role: "toolResult",
 183 | |                       toolCallId: tc.id,
 184 | |                       toolName: tc.name,
 185 | |                       content: [{ type: "text", text: "aborted" }],
 186 | |                       isError: true,
 187 | |                       timestamp: pendingAbortedTimestamp,
 188 | |                   } as ToolResultMessage);
 189 | |                   toolCallStatus.set(tc.id, ToolCallStatus.Aborted);
 190 | |               }
 191 | |           }
 192 | |           result.push({
 193 | |               role: "developer",
 194 | |               content: turnAbortedGuidance,
 195 | |               timestamp: pendingAbortedTimestamp + 1,
 196 | |           } as DeveloperMessage);
 197 | |           pendingAbortedToolCalls = new Map();
 198 | |           pendingAbortedTimestamp = undefined;
 199 | |       };
 200 | |   
 201 | |       for (let i = 0; i < transformed.length; i++) {
 202 | |           const msg = transformed[i];
 203 | |           const messageTimestamp = "timestamp" in msg && typeof msg.timestamp === "number" ? msg.timestamp : Date.now();
 204 | |   
 205 | |           if (msg.role === "assistant") {
 206 | |               flushPendingToolCalls(messageTimestamp);
 207 | |               flushPendingAbortedToolCalls();
 208 | |   
 209 | |               const assistantMsg = msg as AssistantMessage;
 210 | |               const toolCalls = assistantMsg.content.filter(b => b.type === "toolCall") as ToolCall[];
 211 | |   
 212 | |               if (assistantMsg.stopReason === "error" || assistantMsg.stopReason === "aborted") {
 213 | |                   // Keep the assistant message with tool calls intact. If real tool results follow, preserve them;
 214 | |                   // otherwise synthesize aborted results before the next turn boundary.
 215 | |                   result.push(msg);
 216 | |                   pendingAbortedToolCalls = new Map(toolCalls.map(toolCall => [toolCall.id, toolCall] as const));
 217 | |                   pendingAbortedTimestamp = assistantMsg.timestamp;
 218 | |                   continue;
 219 | |               }
 220 | |   
 221 | |               if (toolCalls.length > 0) {
 222 | |                   pendingToolCalls = toolCalls;
 223 | |               }
 224 | |           } else if (msg.role === "toolResult") {
 225 | |               if (pendingAbortedToolCalls.has(msg.toolCallId)) {
 226 | |                   pendingAbortedToolCalls.delete(msg.toolCallId);
 227 | |               } else if (toolCallStatus.get(msg.toolCallId) === ToolCallStatus.Aborted) {
 228 | |                   continue;
 229 | |               }
 230 | |               toolCallStatus.set(msg.toolCallId, ToolCallStatus.Resolved);
 231 | |           } else {
 232 | |               flushPendingToolCalls(messageTimestamp);
 233 | |               flushPendingAbortedToolCalls();
 234 | |           }
 235 | |   
 236 | |           result.push(msg);
 237 | |       }
 238 | |   
 239 | |       flushPendingToolCalls(Date.now());
 240 | |       flushPendingAbortedToolCalls();
 241 | |   
 242 | |       return result;
 243 | `-> }

  77 | |       const eventType = typeof rawEvent.type === "string" ? rawEvent.type : "";
  78 | |       if (eventType === "") return args.firstTokenTime;

 277 | ,-> export function enforceStrictSchema(

 289 | |           return cached;

 312 | |                           : value;

 314 | |                   if (!originalRequired.has(key)) {

 324 | |                   }

 330 | |       }

 343 | |           if (Array.isArray(result[key])) {
 344 | |               result[key] = (result[key] as unknown[]).map(entry =>

 154 | |                       propertyName,
 155 | |                       isJsonObject(propertySchema) ? sanitizeSchemaForStrictMode(propertySchema, seen, cache) : propertySchema,
 156 | |                   ]),
 157 | |               );
 158 | |               sanitized.properties = properties;
 159 | |               continue;
 160 | |           }
 161 | |   
 162 | |           if (key === "items") {
 163 | |               if (isJsonObject(value)) {
 164 | |                   sanitized.items = sanitizeSchemaForStrictMode(value, seen, cache);
 165 | |               } else if (Array.isArray(value)) {
 166 | |                   sanitized.items = value.map(entry =>
 167 | |                       isJsonObject(entry) ? sanitizeSchemaForStrictMode(entry, seen, cache) : entry,
 168 | |                   );
 169 | |               } else {
 170 | |                   sanitized.items = value;
 171 | |               }
 172 | |               continue;
 173 | |           }
 174 | |   
 175 | |           if (COMBINATOR_KEYS.includes(key as (typeof COMBINATOR_KEYS)[number]) && Array.isArray(value)) {
 176 | |               sanitized[key] = value.map(entry =>
 177 | |                   isJsonObject(entry) ? sanitizeSchemaForStrictMode(entry, seen, cache) : entry,
 178 | |               );
 179 | |               continue;
 180 | |           }
 181 | |   
 182 | |           if ((key === "$defs" || key === "definitions") && isJsonObject(value)) {
 183 | |               sanitized[key] = Object.fromEntries(
 184 | |                   Object.entries(value).map(([definitionName, definitionSchema]) => [
 185 | |                       definitionName,
 186 | |                       isJsonObject(definitionSchema)
 187 | |                           ? sanitizeSchemaForStrictMode(definitionSchema, seen, cache)
 188 | |                           : definitionSchema,
 189 | |                   ]),
 190 | |               );
 191 | |               continue;
 192 | |           }
 193 | |   
 194 | |           if (key === "additionalProperties") {
 195 | |               continue;
 196 | |           }
 197 | |   
 198 | |           if (key === "description" && typeof value === "string" && schema.default !== undefined) {
 199 | |               // Preserve `default:` info for strict-mode providers that strip the keyword.
 200 | |               // Inline as `(default: X)` text in the description, matching the convention for
 201 | |               // runtime-placeholder defaults (e.g. `cwd`) that cannot live in the keyword form.
 202 | |               const defaultVal = schema.default;
 203 | |               const formatted = typeof defaultVal === "string" ? defaultVal : JSON.stringify(defaultVal);
 204 | |               sanitized.description = value.includes("(default:") ? value : `${value} (default: ${formatted})`;
 205 | |               continue;
 206 | |           }
 207 | |   
 208 | |           sanitized[key] = value;
 209 | |       }
 210 | |   
 211 | |       if (Object.hasOwn(schema, "const")) {
 212 | |           const constVal = schema.const;
 213 | |           const existingEnum = Array.isArray(sanitized.enum) ? sanitized.enum : [];
 214 | |           if (!existingEnum.some(v => areJsonValuesEqual(v, constVal))) {
 215 | |               existingEnum.push(constVal);
 216 | |           }
 217 | |           sanitized.enum = existingEnum;
 218 | |       }
 219 | |   
 220 | |       if (typeof typeValue === "string") {
 221 | |           sanitized.type = typeValue;
 222 | |       }
 223 | |   
 224 | |       if (sanitized.type === undefined && isJsonObject(sanitized.properties)) {
 225 | |           sanitized.type = "object";
 226 | |       }
 227 | |   
 228 | |       if (sanitized.type === undefined && sanitized.items !== undefined) {
 229 | |           sanitized.type = "array";
 230 | |       }
 231 | |   
 232 | |       if (sanitized.type === undefined && Array.isArray(sanitized.enum)) {
 233 | |           const enumTypes = new Set(
 234 | |               sanitized.enum
 235 | |                   .map(v =>
 236 | |                       v === null
 237 | |                           ? "null"
 238 | |                           : typeof v === "string"
 239 | |                               ? "string"
 240 | |                               : typeof v === "number"
 241 | |                                   ? "number"
 242 | |                                   : typeof v === "boolean"
 243 | |                                       ? "boolean"
 244 | |                                       : undefined,
 245 | |                   )
 246 | |                   .filter((t): t is "null" | "string" | "number" | "boolean" => t !== undefined),
 247 | |           );
 248 | |           if (enumTypes.size === 1) {
 249 | |               sanitized.type = [...enumTypes][0];
 250 | |           }
 251 | |       }
 252 | |   
 253 | |       if (schema.nullable === true) {
 254 | |           const { nullable: _, ...withoutNullable } = sanitized;
 255 | |           seen.delete(schema);
 256 | |           return { anyOf: [withoutNullable, { type: "null" }] };
 257 | |       }
 258 | |   
 259 | |       seen.delete(schema);
 260 | |       return sanitized;

 278 | |       schema: Record<string, unknown>,
 279 | |       seen?: WeakSet<object>,
 280 | |       cache?: WeakMap<Record<string, unknown>, Record<string, unknown>>,
 281 | |   ): Record<string, unknown> {
 282 | |       if (!seen) seen = new WeakSet();
 283 | |       if (!cache) cache = new WeakMap();
 284 | |       if (seen.has(schema)) {
 285 | |           throw new Error("Schema contains a circular object graph — cannot enforce strict mode");
 286 | |       }
 287 | |       const cached = cache.get(schema);
 288 | |       if (cached) {
 289 | |           return cached;
 290 | |       }
 291 | |       seen.add(schema);
 292 | |       const result = { ...schema };
 293 | |       cache.set(schema, result);
 294 | |       const isObjectType = result.type === "object";
 295 | |       if (isObjectType) {
 296 | |           result.additionalProperties = false;
 297 | |           const propertiesValue = result.properties;
 298 | |           const props =
 299 | |               propertiesValue !== null && typeof propertiesValue === "object" && !Array.isArray(propertiesValue)
 300 | |                   ? (propertiesValue as Record<string, unknown>)
 301 | |                   : {};

 303 | |               Array.isArray(result.required)
 304 | |                   ? result.required.filter((value): value is string => typeof value === "string")
 305 | |                   : [],
 306 | |           );
 307 | |           const strictProperties = Object.fromEntries(
 308 | |               Object.entries(props).map(([key, value]) => {
 309 | |                   const processed =
 310 | |                       value !== null && typeof value === "object" && !Array.isArray(value)
 311 | |                           ? enforceStrictSchema(value as Record<string, unknown>, seen, cache)
 312 | |                           : value;
 313 | |                   // Optional property — wrap as nullable so strict mode accepts it
 314 | |                   if (!originalRequired.has(key)) {
 315 | |                       // Don't double-wrap if already nullable
 316 | |                       if (
 317 | |                           isJsonObject(processed) &&

 320 | |                       ) {
 321 | |                           return [key, processed];
 322 | |                       }
 323 | |                       return [key, { anyOf: [processed, { type: "null" }] }];
 324 | |                   }
 325 | |                   return [key, processed];
 326 | |               }),
 327 | |           );
 328 | |           result.properties = strictProperties;
 329 | |           result.required = Object.keys(strictProperties);
 330 | |       }
 331 | |       if (result.items !== null && typeof result.items === "object") {
 332 | |           if (Array.isArray(result.items)) {
 333 | |               result.items = result.items.map(entry =>
 334 | |                   entry !== null && typeof entry === "object" && !Array.isArray(entry)
 335 | |                       ? enforceStrictSchema(entry as Record<string, unknown>, seen, cache)
 336 | |                       : entry,
 337 | |               );
 338 | |           } else {
 339 | |               result.items = enforceStrictSchema(result.items as Record<string, unknown>, seen, cache);
 340 | |           }
 341 | |       }
 342 | |       for (const key of COMBINATOR_KEYS) {
 343 | |           if (Array.isArray(result[key])) {
 344 | |               result[key] = (result[key] as unknown[]).map(entry =>
 345 | |                   entry !== null && typeof entry === "object" && !Array.isArray(entry)
 346 | |                       ? enforceStrictSchema(entry as Record<string, unknown>, seen, cache)
 347 | |                       : entry,
 348 | |               );
 349 | |           }
 350 | |       }

 359 | |                           : def,
 360 | |                   ]),
 361 | |               );
 362 | |           }
 363 | |       }
 364 | |       // Strict mode requires every schema node to declare a concrete type (or combinator/$ref).
 365 | |       // Schemas like `{}` (match anything) or `{items: {}}` are not representable in strict mode.
 366 | |       if (
 367 | |           result.type === undefined &&

 372 | |           throw new Error("Schema node has no type, combinator, or $ref — cannot enforce strict mode");

 374 | |       seen.delete(schema);

 433 | |                   }
 434 | |                   currentItem.summary.push(event.part);
 435 | |               }
 436 | |           } else if (event.type === "response.reasoning_summary_text.delta") {
 437 | |               if (currentItem?.type === "reasoning" && currentBlock?.type === "thinking") {
 438 | |                   if (currentItem.summary === undefined || currentItem.summary === null) {
 439 | |                       currentItem.summary = [];
 440 | |                   }

 442 | |                   if (lastPart !== undefined && lastPart !== null) {
 443 | |                       currentBlock.thinking += event.delta;
 444 | |                       lastPart.text += event.delta;

 446 | |                           type: "thinking_delta",
 447 | |                           contentIndex: blockIndex(),
 448 | |                           delta: event.delta,
 449 | |                           partial: output,
 450 | |                       });
 451 | |                   }
 452 | |               }
 453 | |           } else if (event.type === "response.reasoning_summary_part.done") {
 454 | |               if (currentItem?.type === "reasoning" && currentBlock?.type === "thinking") {
 455 | |                   if (currentItem.summary === undefined || currentItem.summary === null) {
 456 | |                       currentItem.summary = [];
 457 | |                   }
 458 | |                   const lastPart = currentItem.summary[currentItem.summary.length - 1];
 459 | |                   if (lastPart !== undefined && lastPart !== null) {
 460 | |                       currentBlock.thinking += "\n\n";
 461 | |                       lastPart.text += "\n\n";
 462 | |                       stream.push({
 463 | |                           type: "thinking_delta",
 464 | |                           contentIndex: blockIndex(),

 466 | |                           partial: output,
 467 | |                       });
 468 | |                   }
 469 | |               }
 470 | |           } else if (event.type === "response.reasoning_text.delta") {
 471 | |               if (currentItem?.type === "reasoning" && currentBlock?.type === "thinking") {
 472 | |                   currentBlock.thinking += event.delta;
 473 | |                   stream.push({
 474 | |                       type: "thinking_delta",
 475 | |                       contentIndex: blockIndex(),
 476 | |                       delta: event.delta,
 477 | |                       partial: output,
 478 | |                   });
 479 | |               }
 480 | |           } else if (event.type === "response.content_part.added") {
 481 | |               if (currentItem?.type === "message") {
 482 | |                   if (currentItem.content === undefined || currentItem.content === null) {
 483 | |                       currentItem.content = [];
 484 | |                   }
 485 | |                   if (event.part.type === "output_text" || event.part.type === "refusal") {
 486 | |                       currentItem.content.push(event.part);

 488 | |               }

 492 | |                   if (lastPart?.type === "output_text") {

 499 | |                           partial: output,
 500 | |                       });
 501 | |                   }
 502 | |               }

 516 | |               }

 520 | |                   currentBlock.arguments = (parseStreamingJson(currentBlock.partialJson) ?? {}) as Record<string, unknown>;
 521 | |                   stream.push({
 522 | |                       type: "toolcall_delta",
 523 | |                       contentIndex: blockIndex(),
 524 | |                       delta: event.delta,
 525 | |                       partial: output,
 526 | |                   });
 527 | |               }
 528 | |           } else if (event.type === "response.function_call_arguments.done") {
 529 | |               if (currentItem?.type === "function_call" && currentBlock?.type === "toolCall") {
 530 | |                   currentBlock.partialJson = event.arguments;
 531 | |                   currentBlock.arguments = (parseStreamingJson(currentBlock.partialJson) ?? {}) as Record<string, unknown>;
 532 | |               }
 533 | |           } else if (event.type === "response.custom_tool_call_input.delta") {
 534 | |               if (currentItem?.type === "custom_tool_call" && currentBlock?.type === "toolCall") {
 535 | |                   currentBlock.partialJson += event.delta;

 538 | |                       type: "toolcall_delta",

 541 | |                       partial: output,

 545 | |               if (currentItem?.type === "custom_tool_call" && currentBlock?.type === "toolCall") {
 546 | |                   currentBlock.partialJson = event.input;
 547 | |                   currentBlock.arguments = { input: event.input };
 548 | |               }

 556 | |                           : (item.content?.[0]?.type === "reasoning_text"

 558 | |                               : "");

 561 | |                   ) as ThinkingContent | undefined;
 562 | |                   if (reasoningBlock !== undefined && reasoningBlock !== null) {

 564 | |                       reasoningBlock.thinkingSignature = JSON.stringify(item);
 565 | |                       const reasoningBlockIndex = output.content.indexOf(reasoningBlock);
 566 | |                       stream.push({
 567 | |                           type: "thinking_end",
 568 | |                           contentIndex: reasoningBlockIndex,
 569 | |                           content: thinking,
 570 | |                           partial: output,
 571 | |                       });
 572 | |                   }
 573 | |                   if ((currentBlock as ThinkingContent | null)?.itemId === item.id) currentBlock = null;
 574 | |               } else if (item.type === "message" && currentBlock?.type === "text") {
 575 | |                   currentBlock.text = item.content
 576 | |                       .map(part => (part.type === "output_text" ? (part.text ?? "") : (part.refusal ?? "")))
 577 | |                       .join("");

 579 | |                   stream.push({
 580 | |                       type: "text_end",
 581 | |                       contentIndex: blockIndex(),
 582 | |                       content: currentBlock.text,
 583 | |                       partial: output,
 584 | |                   });
 585 | |                   currentBlock = null;
 586 | |               } else if (item.type === "function_call") {
 587 | |                   const args =
 588 | |                       currentBlock?.type === "toolCall" && currentBlock.partialJson
 589 | |                           ? ((parseStreamingJson(currentBlock.partialJson) ?? {}) as Record<string, unknown>)
 590 | |                           : ((parseStreamingJson(item.arguments || "{}") ?? {}) as Record<string, unknown>);
 591 | |                   const toolCall: ToolCall = {
 592 | |                       type: "toolCall",
 593 | |                       id: encodeResponsesToolCallId(item.call_id, item.id),
 594 | |                       name: item.name,
 595 | |                       arguments: args,
 596 | |                   };
 597 | |                   currentBlock = null;
 598 | |                   stream.push({ type: "toolcall_end", contentIndex: blockIndex(), toolCall, partial: output });
 599 | |               } else if (item.type === "custom_tool_call") {
 600 | |                   const rawInput =
 601 | |                       currentBlock?.type === "toolCall" && currentBlock.partialJson
 602 | |                           ? currentBlock.partialJson
 603 | |                           : (item.input ?? "");
 604 | |                   const toolCall: ToolCall = {
 605 | |                       type: "toolCall",

 608 | |                       arguments: { input: rawInput },

 612 | |                   stream.push({ type: "toolcall_end", contentIndex: blockIndex(), toolCall, partial: output });
 613 | |               }
 614 | |           } else if (event.type === "response.completed") {
 615 | |               const response = event.response;
 616 | |               if (response?.id !== undefined && response.id !== null && response.id !== "") {
 617 | |                   output.responseId = response.id;
 618 | |               }

 622 | |                   output.usage = {
 623 | |                       input: (response.usage.input_tokens || 0) - cachedTokens,
 624 | |                       output: response.usage.output_tokens || 0,
 625 | |                       cacheRead: cachedTokens,
 626 | |                       cacheWrite: 0,
 627 | |                       totalTokens: response.usage.total_tokens || 0,
 628 | |                       ...(reasoningTokens > 0 ? { reasoningTokens } : {}),
 629 | |                       cost: { input: 0, output: 0, cacheRead: 0, cacheWrite: 0, total: 0 },
 630 | |                   };
 631 | |               }
 632 | |               calculateCost(model, output.usage);
 633 | |               output.stopReason = mapOpenAIResponsesStopReason(response?.status);
 634 | |               if (output.content.some(block => block.type === "toolCall") && output.stopReason === "stop") {
 635 | |                   output.stopReason = "toolUse";
 636 | |               }
 637 | |           } else if (event.type === "error") {
 638 | |               throw new Error(`Error Code ${event.code}: ${event.message}` || "Unknown error");
 639 | |           } else if (event.type === "response.failed") {
 640 | |               const error = event.response?.error;
 641 | |               const details = event.response?.incomplete_details;

 643 | |                   ? `${error.code || "unknown"}: ${error.message || "no message"}`
 644 | |                   : (details?.reason
 645 | |                       ? `incomplete: ${details.reason}`
 646 | |                       : "Unknown error (no error details in response)");
 647 | |               throw new Error(message);
 648 | |           }
 649 | |       }

  ! eslint(complexity): function `convertResponsesAssistantMessage` has a complexity of 30. Maximum allowed is 20.
     ,-[packages/ai/src/providers/openai-responses-shared.ts:232:8]
 231 |     
 232 | ,-> export function convertResponsesAssistantMessage<TApi extends Api>(
 233 | |       assistantMsg: AssistantMessage,
 234 | |       model: Model<TApi>,
 235 | |       msgIndex: number,
 236 | |       knownCallIds: Set<string>,
 237 | |       includeThinkingSignatures = true,
 238 | |       customCallIds?: Set<string>,
 239 | |   ): ResponseInput {
 240 | |       const outputItems: ResponseInput = [];
 241 | |       const isDifferentModel =
 242 | |           assistantMsg.model !== model.id && assistantMsg.provider === model.provider && assistantMsg.api === model.api;
 243 | |   
 244 | |       for (const block of assistantMsg.content) {
 245 | |           if (block.type === "thinking" && assistantMsg.stopReason !== "error") {
 246 | |               if (!includeThinkingSignatures) {
 247 | |                   continue;
 248 | |               }
 249 | |               if (
 250 | |                   block.thinkingSignature !== null &&
 251 | |                   block.thinkingSignature !== undefined &&
 252 | |                   block.thinkingSignature !== ""
 253 | |               ) {
 254 | |                   outputItems.push(JSON.parse(block.thinkingSignature) as ResponseReasoningItem);
 255 | |               }
 256 | |               continue;
 257 | |           }
 258 | |   
 259 | |           if (block.type === "text") {
 260 | |               const parsedSignature = parseTextSignature(block.textSignature);
 261 | |               let msgId = parsedSignature?.id;
 262 | |               if (msgId === null || msgId === undefined || msgId === "") {
 263 | |                   msgId = `msg_${msgIndex}`;
 264 | |               } else if (msgId.length > 64) {
 265 | |                   msgId = `msg_${Bun.hash(msgId).toString(36)}`;
 266 | |               }
 267 | |               outputItems.push({
 268 | |                   type: "message",
 269 | |                   role: "assistant",
 270 | |                   content: [{ type: "output_text", text: block.text.toWellFormed(), annotations: [] }],
 271 | |                   status: "completed",
 272 | |                   id: msgId,
 273 | |                   phase: parsedSignature?.phase,
 274 | |               } satisfies ResponseOutputMessage);
 275 | |               continue;
 276 | |           }
 277 | |   
 278 | |           if (block.type !== "toolCall") {
 279 | |               continue;
 280 | |           }
 281 | |   
 282 | |           const normalized = normalizeResponsesToolCallId(block.id);
 283 | |           let itemId: string | undefined = normalized.itemId;
 284 | |           if (isDifferentModel && (itemId?.startsWith("fc_") || itemId?.startsWith("fcr_"))) {
 285 | |               itemId = undefined;
 286 | |           }
 287 | |           knownCallIds.add(normalized.callId);
 288 | |           if (block.customWireName !== null && block.customWireName !== undefined && block.customWireName !== "") {
 289 | |               const rawInput = typeof block.arguments?.input === "string" ? block.arguments.input : "";
 290 | |               customCallIds?.add(normalized.callId);
 291 | |               outputItems.push({
 292 | |                   type: "custom_tool_call",
 293 | |                   id: itemId,
 294 | |                   call_id: normalized.callId,
 295 | |                   name: block.customWireName,
 296 | |                   input: rawInput,
 297 | |               } as ResponseInput[number]);
 298 | |               continue;
 299 | |           }
 300 | |           outputItems.push({
 301 | |               type: "function_call",
 302 | |               id: itemId,
 303 | |               call_id: normalized.callId,
 304 | |               name: block.name,
 305 | |               arguments: JSON.stringify(block.arguments),
 306 | |           });
 307 | |       }
 308 | |   
 309 | |       return outputItems;
 310 | `-> }

  20 | ,-> function mergeObjectCombinerVariants(schema: JsonObject, combiner: "anyOf" | "oneOf"): JsonObject {
  21 | |       const variantsRaw = schema[combiner];
  22 | |       if (!Array.isArray(variantsRaw) || variantsRaw.length === 0) {
  23 | |           return schema;
  24 | |       }
  25 | |   
  26 | |       const variants: JsonObject[] = [];
  27 | |       for (const entry of variantsRaw) {
  28 | |           if (!isJsonObject(entry)) {
  29 | |               return schema;
  30 | |           }
  31 | |           const variantType = entry.type;
  32 | |           const hasObjectShape =
  33 | |               isJsonObject(entry.properties) ||
  34 | |               Array.isArray(entry.required) ||
  35 | |               Object.hasOwn(entry, "additionalProperties");
  36 | |           if (variantType === undefined && !hasObjectShape) {
  37 | |               return schema;
  38 | |           }
  39 | |           if (variantType !== undefined && variantType !== "object") {
  40 | |               return schema;
  41 | |           }
  42 | |           if (entry.properties !== undefined && !isJsonObject(entry.properties)) {
  43 | |               return schema;
  44 | |           }
  45 | |           if (entry.required !== undefined && !Array.isArray(entry.required)) {
  46 | |               return schema;
  47 | |           }
  48 | |           variants.push(entry);
  49 | |       }
  50 | |   
  51 | |       const mergedProperties: JsonObject = {};
  52 | |       const ownProperties = isJsonObject(schema.properties) ? schema.properties : {};
  53 | |       for (const [name, propertySchema] of Object.entries(ownProperties)) {
  54 | |           mergedProperties[name] = propertySchema;
  55 | |       }
  56 | |   
  57 | |       for (const variant of variants) {
  58 | |           const properties = isJsonObject(variant.properties) ? variant.properties : {};
  59 | |           for (const [name, propertySchema] of Object.entries(properties)) {
  60 | |               const existingSchema = mergedProperties[name];
  61 | |               mergedProperties[name] =
  62 | |                   existingSchema === undefined ? propertySchema : mergePropertySchemas(existingSchema, propertySchema);
  63 | |           }
  64 | |       }
  65 | |   
  66 | |       const nextSchema = copySchemaWithout(schema, combiner);
  67 | |   
  68 | |       nextSchema.type = "object";
  69 | |       nextSchema.properties = mergedProperties;
  70 | |   
  71 | |       // Compute intersection of all variants' required arrays
  72 | |       let requiredIntersection: string[] | undefined;
  73 | |       for (const variant of variants) {
  74 | |           const variantRequired = Array.isArray(variant.required)
  75 | |               ? variant.required.filter((r): r is string => typeof r === "string")
  76 | |               : [];
  77 | |           if (requiredIntersection === undefined) {
  78 | |               requiredIntersection = [...variantRequired];
  79 | |           } else {
  80 | |               const reqSet = new Set(variantRequired);
  81 | |               requiredIntersection = requiredIntersection.filter(r => reqSet.has(r));
  82 | |           }
  83 | |       }
  84 | |       const parentRequired = Array.isArray(schema.required)
  85 | |           ? schema.required.filter((r): r is string => typeof r === "string")
  86 | |           : [];
  87 | |       const ownPropertyNames = new Set(Object.keys(ownProperties));
  88 | |       const safeRequired = new Set<string>();
  89 | |       for (const name of requiredIntersection ?? []) {
  90 | |           if (name in mergedProperties) safeRequired.add(name);
  91 | |       }
  92 | |       for (const name of parentRequired) {
  93 | |           if (ownPropertyNames.has(name) && name in mergedProperties) {
  94 | |               safeRequired.add(name);
  95 | |           }
  96 | |       }
  97 | |       const requiredInPropertyOrder = Object.keys(mergedProperties).filter(name => safeRequired.has(name));
  98 | |       if (requiredInPropertyOrder.length > 0) {
  99 | |           nextSchema.required = requiredInPropertyOrder;
 100 | |       } else {
 101 | |           delete nextSchema.required;
 102 | |       }
 103 | |   
 104 | |       return nextSchema;

  x eslint(complexity): function `collapseMixedTypeCombinerVariants` has a complexity of 21. Maximum allowed is 12.
     ,-[packages/ai/src/utils/schema/normalize-cca.ts:113:1]
 112 |      */
 113 | ,-> function collapseMixedTypeCombinerVariants(schema: JsonObject, combiner: "anyOf" | "oneOf"): JsonObject {
 114 | |       const variantsRaw = schema[combiner];
 115 | |       if (!Array.isArray(variantsRaw) || variantsRaw.length === 0) {
 116 | |           return schema;
 117 | |       }
 118 | |   
 119 | |       const seenTypes = new Set<string>();
 120 | |       const variantTypes: string[] = [];
 121 | |       const mergedVariantFields: JsonObject = {};
 122 | |       for (const entry of variantsRaw) {
 123 | |           if (!isJsonObject(entry) || typeof entry.type !== "string") {
 124 | |               return schema;
 125 | |           }
 126 | |   
 127 | |           const variantType = entry.type;
 128 | |           if (seenTypes.has(variantType)) {
 129 | |               return schema;
 130 | |           }
 131 | |   
 132 | |           const allowedKeys = CLOUD_CODE_ASSIST_TYPE_SPECIFIC_KEYS[variantType];
 133 | |           if (!allowedKeys) {
 134 | |               return schema;
 135 | |           }
 136 | |   
 137 | |           for (const [key, variantValue] of Object.entries(entry)) {
 138 | |               if (key === "type") continue;
 139 | |               if (!allowedKeys.has(key) && !CLOUD_CODE_ASSIST_SHARED_SCHEMA_KEYS.has(key)) {
 140 | |                   return schema;
 141 | |               }
 142 | |   
 143 | |               const existingValue = mergedVariantFields[key];
 144 | |               if (existingValue !== undefined && !areJsonValuesEqual(existingValue, variantValue)) {
 145 | |                   return schema;
 146 | |               }
 147 | |               mergedVariantFields[key] = variantValue;
 148 | |           }
 149 | |   
 150 | |           seenTypes.add(variantType);
 151 | |           variantTypes.push(variantType);
 152 | |       }
 153 | |   
 154 | |       if (variantTypes.length < 2 || variantTypes.every(type => type === "object")) {
 155 | |           return schema;
 156 | |       }
 157 | |   
 158 | |       const nextSchema = copySchemaWithout(schema, combiner);
 159 | |   
 160 | |       const nonNullTypes = variantTypes.filter(t => t !== "null");
 161 | |       // Lossy: when multiple non-null types exist we pick the first. CCA requires
 162 | |       // a scalar type and keeping the anyOf would cause an API rejection at runtime.

 168 | |           }
 169 | |           if (existingValue === undefined) {

 271 | ,-> function extractNullableUnionSchema(schema: unknown): NullableExtractionResult {
 272 | |       if (!isJsonObject(schema)) {
 273 | |           return { schema, nullable: false };
 274 | |       }
 275 | |   
 276 | |       if (schema.nullable === true) {
 277 | |           const nextSchema = { ...schema };
 278 | |           delete nextSchema.nullable;
 279 | |           return { schema: nextSchema, nullable: true };
 280 | |       }
 281 | |   
 282 | |       if (Array.isArray(schema.type)) {
 283 | |           const typeVariants = schema.type.filter((entry): entry is string => typeof entry === "string");
 284 | |           const nonNullTypes = typeVariants.filter(entry => entry !== "null");
 285 | |           if (typeVariants.includes("null") && nonNullTypes.length === 1) {
 286 | |               const nextSchema = { ...schema, type: nonNullTypes[0] };
 287 | |               return { schema: nextSchema, nullable: true };
 288 | |           }
 289 | |       }
 290 | |   
 291 | |       for (const combiner of ["anyOf", "oneOf"] as const) {
 292 | |           const variantsRaw = schema[combiner];
 293 | |           if (!Array.isArray(variantsRaw)) continue;
 294 | |   
 295 | |           let hasNullVariant = false;
 296 | |           const nonNullVariants: unknown[] = [];
 297 | |           for (const variant of variantsRaw) {
 298 | |               if (isJsonObject(variant) && variant.type === "null" && Object.keys(variant).length === 1) {
 299 | |                   hasNullVariant = true;
 300 | |                   continue;
 301 | |               }
 302 | |               nonNullVariants.push(variant);
 303 | |           }
 304 | |   
 305 | |           if (!hasNullVariant || nonNullVariants.length !== 1 || !isJsonObject(nonNullVariants[0])) {
 306 | |               continue;
 307 | |           }
 308 | |   
 309 | |           const nextSchema = copySchemaWithout(schema, combiner);
 310 | |           for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(nonNullVariants[0])) {
 311 | |               const existingValue = nextSchema[key];
 312 | |               if (existingValue !== undefined && !areJsonValuesEqual(existingValue, value)) {
 313 | |                   return { schema, nullable: false };
 314 | |               }
 315 | |               if (existingValue === undefined) {
 316 | |                   nextSchema[key] = value;
 317 | |               }
 318 | |           }
 319 | |           return { schema: nextSchema, nullable: true };

 321 | |

  70 | ,-> export async function* iterateWithIdleTimeout<T>(

  72 | |       options: IdleTimeoutIteratorOptions,
  73 | |   ): AsyncGenerator<T> {
  74 | |       let watchdog = options.watchdog;
  75 | |       const firstItemTimeoutMs = options.firstItemTimeoutMs ?? options.idleTimeoutMs;
  76 | |       if (
  77 | |           (firstItemTimeoutMs === undefined || firstItemTimeoutMs <= 0) &&
  78 | |           (options.idleTimeoutMs === undefined || options.idleTimeoutMs <= 0)
  79 | |       ) {
  80 | |           for await (const item of iterable) {
  81 | |               watchdog && clearTimeout(watchdog);
  82 | |               watchdog = undefined;
  83 | |               yield item;
  84 | |           }
  85 | |           return;
  86 | |       }
  87 | |   
  88 | |       const iterator = iterable[Symbol.asyncIterator]();
  89 | |   
  90 | |       const withRacy = <T>(promise: Promise<T>) =>
  91 | |           promise.then(
  92 | |               result => ({ kind: "next" as const, result }),
  93 | |               error => ({ kind: "error" as const, error }),
  94 | |           );
  95 | |   
  96 | |       let onFirst: (() => void) | null = () => {
  97 | |           if (watchdog !== undefined && watchdog !== null) clearTimeout(watchdog);
  98 | |           onFirst = null;
  99 | |       };
 100 | |   
 101 | |       while (true) {
 102 | |           const nextResultPromise = withRacy(iterator.next());

 104 | |   
 105 | |           if (activeTimeoutMs === undefined || activeTimeoutMs <= 0) {
 106 | |               const outcome = await nextResultPromise;
 107 | |               if (outcome.kind === "error") {
 108 | |                   throw outcome.error;
 109 | |               }
 110 | |               if (outcome.result.done === true) {
 111 | |                   return;
 112 | |               }
 113 | |               onFirst?.();
 114 | |               yield outcome.result.value;
 115 | |               continue;
 116 | |           }
 117 | |   
 118 | |           const { promise: timeoutPromise, resolve: resolveTimeout } = Promise.withResolvers<{
 119 | |               kind: "timeout";
 120 | |           }>();
 121 | |           const timer = setTimeout(() => resolveTimeout({ kind: "timeout" }), activeTimeoutMs);
 122 | |   
 123 | |           try {
 124 | |               const outcome = await Promise.race([nextResultPromise, timeoutPromise]);
 125 | |               if (outcome.kind === "timeout") {
 126 | |                   if (onFirst === null) {
 127 | |                       options.onIdle?.();
 128 | |                   } else {
 129 | |                       options.onFirstItemTimeout?.();
 130 | |                   }

 132 | |                   if (returnPromise !== undefined && returnPromise !== null) {
 133 | |                       void returnPromise.catch(() => {});
 134 | |                   }
 135 | |                   throw new Error(
 136 | |                       onFirst === null ? options.errorMessage : (options.firstItemErrorMessage ?? options.errorMessage),
 137 | |                   );
 138 | |               }
 139 | |               if (watchdog !== undefined && watchdog !== null) clearTimeout(watchdog);
 140 | |               watchdog = undefined;
 141 | |               if (outcome.kind === "error") {
 142 | |                   throw outcome.error;
 143 | |               }
 144 | |               if (outcome.result.done === true) {
 145 | |                   return;
 146 | |               }
 147 | |               onFirst?.();

 181 | |                   isOAuth: isOAuthToken(storedApiKey),

 183 | |           }

 167 | ,-> async function pollForToken(
 168 | |       deviceCode: string,
 169 | |       intervalMs: number,
 170 | |       expiresInMs: number,
 171 | |       signal?: AbortSignal,
 172 | |   ): Promise<OAuthCredentials> {
 173 | |       const deadline = Date.now() + expiresInMs;
 174 | |       let waitMs = Math.max(1000, intervalMs);
 175 | |   
 176 | |       while (Date.now() < deadline) {
 177 | |           if (signal !== undefined && signal.aborted) {
 178 | |               throw new Error("Login cancelled");
 179 | |           }
 180 | |

 200 | |           ) {

 202 | |           }

 205 | |           if (error === "authorization_pending") {
 206 | |               await abortableSleep(waitMs, signal);
 207 | |               continue;
 208 | |           }

 211 | |               waitMs += 5000;
 212 | |               const retryAfter = typeof payload.interval === "number" ? payload.interval * 1000 : undefined;
 213 | |               if (retryAfter !== null && retryAfter !== undefined && retryAfter !== 0 && retryAfter > waitMs)

 215 | |               await abortableSleep(waitMs, signal);
 216 | |               continue;
 217 | |           }
 218 | |

 608 | |           if (!$env.OPENAI_API_KEY) {
 609 | |               throw new Error(
 610 | |                   "OpenAI API key is required. Set OPENAI_API_KEY environment variable or pass it as an argument.",
 611 | |               );
 612 | |           }
 613 | |           apiKey = $env.OPENAI_API_KEY;
 614 | |       }

 617 | |       if (model.provider === "kimi-code") {
 618 | |           headers = { ...(await getKimiCommonHeaders()), ...headers };
 619 | |       }
 620 | |

 622 | |       let capturedErrorResponse: CapturedHttpErrorResponse | undefined;
 623 | |       const wrappedFetch = Object.assign(
 624 | |           async (input: string | URL | Request, init?: RequestInit): Promise<Response> => {
 625 | |               const response = await fetch(input, init);
 626 | |               if (response.ok) {
 627 | |                   capturedErrorResponse = undefined;
 628 | |                   return response;
 629 | |               }
 630 | |               let bodyText: string | undefined;
 631 | |               let bodyJson: unknown;
 632 | |               try {
 633 | |                   bodyText = await response.clone().text();
 634 | |                   if (bodyText.trim().length > 0) {
 635 | |                       try {
 636 | |                           bodyJson = JSON.parse(bodyText);
 637 | |                       } catch {}
 638 | |                   }
 639 | |               } catch {}
 640 | |               capturedErrorResponse = {
 641 | |                   status: response.status,
 642 | |                   headers: response.headers,
 643 | |                   bodyText,
 644 | |                   bodyJson,
 645 | |               };
 646 | |               return response;
 647 | |           },
 648 | |           { preconnect: fetch.preconnect },
 649 | |       );
 650 | |       return {
 651 | |           client: new OpenAI({
 652 | |               apiKey,
 653 | |               baseURL: baseUrl,
 654 | |               dangerouslyAllowBrowser: true,
 655 | |               maxRetries: 5,
 656 | |               defaultHeaders: headers,
 657 | |               fetch: wrappedFetch,
 658 | |           }),
 659 | |           baseUrl,
 660 | |           requestHeaders: headers,
 661 | |           getCapturedErrorResponse: () => capturedErrorResponse,
 662 | |           clearCapturedErrorResponse: () => {
 663 | |               capturedErrorResponse = undefined;
 664 | |           },
 665 | |       };

  795 | ,-> export function convertMessages(
  796 | |       model: Model<"openai-completions">,

  799 | |   ): ChatCompletionMessageParam[] {
  800 | |       const params: ChatCompletionMessageParam[] = [];
  801 | |   
  802 | |       const normalizeToolCallId = (id: string): string => {
  803 | |           if (compat.requiresMistralToolIds) return normalizeMistralToolId(id, true);
  804 | |   
  805 | |           if (id.includes("|")) {
  806 | |               const [callId] = id.split("|");
  807 | |               return callId.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/g, "_").slice(0, 40);
  808 | |           }
  809 | |   
  810 | |           if (model.provider === "openai") return id.length > 40 ? id.slice(0, 40) : id;
  811 | |           return id;
  812 | |       };
  813 | |       const transformedMessages = transformMessages(context.messages, model, id => normalizeToolCallId(id));
  814 | |   
  815 | |       const remappedToolCallIds = new Map<string, string[]>();
  816 | |       let generatedToolCallIdCounter = 0;
  817 | |   
  818 | |       const generateFallbackToolCallId = (seed: string): string => {
  819 | |           generatedToolCallIdCounter += 1;
  820 | |           const hash = Bun.hash(`${model.provider}:${model.id}:${seed}:${generatedToolCallIdCounter}`).toString(36);
  821 | |           return `call_${hash}`;
  822 | |       };
  823 | |   
  824 | |       const rememberToolCallId = (originalId: string, normalizedId: string): void => {
  825 | |           const queue = remappedToolCallIds.get(originalId);
  826 | |           if (queue) {
  827 | |               queue.push(normalizedId);
  828 | |               return;
  829 | |           }
  830 | |           remappedToolCallIds.set(originalId, [normalizedId]);
  831 | |       };
  832 | |   
  833 | |       const consumeToolCallId = (originalId: string): string | null => {
  834 | |           const queue = remappedToolCallIds.get(originalId);
  835 | |           if (!queue || queue.length === 0) return null;
  836 | |           const nextId = queue.shift() ?? null;
  837 | |           if (queue.length === 0) remappedToolCallIds.delete(originalId);
  838 | |           return nextId;
  839 | |       };
  840 | |   
  841 | |       const ensureToolCallId = (rawId: string, seed: string): string => {

  845 | |       };
  846 | |   
  847 | |       if (context.systemPrompt !== null && context.systemPrompt !== undefined && context.systemPrompt !== "") {

  849 | |           const role = useDeveloperRole ? "developer" : "system";
  850 | |           params.push({ role, content: context.systemPrompt.toWellFormed() });
  851 | |       }
  852 | |   
  853 | |       let lastRole: string | null = null;
  854 | |

  865 | |               });

  867 | |

  869 | |           if (msg.role === "user" || msg.role === "developer") {
  870 | |               const role = !devAsUser && msg.role === "developer" ? "developer" : "user";

  876 | |                       content: text,
  877 | |                   });
  878 | |               } else {

  884 | |                           content.push({
  885 | |                               type: "text",
  886 | |                               text,
  887 | |                           } satisfies ChatCompletionContentPartText);
  888 | |                       } else {
  889 | |                           content.push({
  890 | |                               type: "image_url",
  891 | |                               image_url: {
  892 | |                                   url: `data:${item.mimeType};base64,${item.data}`,
  893 | |                               },
  894 | |                           } satisfies ChatCompletionContentPartImage);

  900 | |                   if (filteredContent.length === 0) continue;
  901 | |                   params.push({
  902 | |                       role: "user",
  903 | |                       content: filteredContent,
  904 | |                   });
  905 | |               }
  906 | |           } else if (msg.role === "assistant") {

  992 | |                   assistantMsg.content = ".";

  994 | |               if (!hasContent && !assistantMsg.tool_calls && !hasReasoningField) {

  x eslint(complexity): function `tryParseLeadingJsonContainer` has a complexity of 18. Maximum allowed is 12.
     ,-[packages/ai/src/utils/validation.ts:94:1]

  94 | ,-> function tryParseLeadingJsonContainer(value: string): unknown | undefined {
  95 | |       const firstChar = value[0];
  96 | |       const closingChar = firstChar === "{" ? "}" : (firstChar === "[" ? "]" : undefined);
  97 | |       if (!closingChar) return undefined;
  98 | |   
  99 | |       let depth = 0;
 100 | |       let inString = false;
 101 | |       let escaped = false;
 102 | |   
 103 | |       for (let index = 0; index < value.length; index += 1) {
 104 | |           const char = value[index];
 105 | |   
 106 | |           if (inString) {
 107 | |               if (escaped) {
 108 | |                   escaped = false;
 109 | |                   continue;
 110 | |               }
 111 | |               if (char === "\\") {
 112 | |                   escaped = true;
 113 | |                   continue;
 114 | |               }
 115 | |               if (char === '"') inString = false;
 116 | |               continue;
 117 | |           }
 118 | |   
 119 | |           if (char === '"') {
 120 | |               inString = true;
 121 | |               continue;
 122 | |           }
 123 | |   
 124 | |           if (char === firstChar) {
 125 | |               depth += 1;
 126 | |               continue;
 127 | |           }
 128 | |   
 129 | |           if (char !== closingChar) continue;
 130 | |           depth -= 1;
 131 | |           if (depth !== 0) continue;
 132 | |   
 133 | |           const prefix = value.slice(0, index + 1);
 134 | |           try {
 135 | |               return JSON.parse(prefix) as unknown;
 136 | |           } catch {
 137 | |               // LLMs sometimes emit literal `\n` or `\t` between JSON tokens
 138 | |               // (e.g. `[{...}\n]`). Convert these to real whitespace and retry.
 139 | |               const cleaned = cleanLiteralEscapes(prefix);
 140 | |               if (cleaned !== prefix) {
 141 | |                   try {
 142 | |                       return JSON.parse(cleaned) as unknown;
 143 | |                   } catch {}
 144 | |               }
 145 | |               // Try escaping raw control chars that appear inside string literals.
 146 | |               const escapedControls = escapeRawControlsInJsonStrings(prefix);
 147 | |               if (escapedControls !== prefix) {
 148 | |                   try {
 149 | |                       return JSON.parse(escapedControls) as unknown;
 150 | |                   } catch {}
 151 | |               }
 152 | |               // Also try single-char healing on the extracted prefix.
 153 | |               return tryHealMalformedJson(prefix);
 154 | |           }
 155 | |       }
 156 | |   
 157 | |       return undefined;
 158 | `-> }

  x eslint(complexity): function `escapeRawControlsInJsonStrings` has a complexity of 14. Maximum allowed is 12.
     ,-[packages/ai/src/utils/validation.ts:211:1]
 210 |      */
 211 | ,-> function escapeRawControlsInJsonStrings(value: string): string {
 212 | |       let result = "";
 213 | |       let inString = false;
 214 | |       let escaped = false;
 215 | |       let changed = false;
 216 | |       for (let i = 0; i < value.length; i += 1) {
 217 | |           const ch = value[i];
 218 | |           if (inString) {
 219 | |               if (escaped) {
 220 | |                   result += ch;
 221 | |                   escaped = false;
 222 | |                   continue;
 223 | |               }
 224 | |               if (ch === "\\") {
 225 | |                   result += ch;
 226 | |                   escaped = true;
 227 | |                   continue;
 228 | |               }
 229 | |               if (ch === '"') {
 230 | |                   result += ch;
 231 | |                   inString = false;
 232 | |                   continue;
 233 | |               }
 234 | |               const code = ch.charCodeAt(0);
 235 | |               if (code < 0x20) {
 236 | |                   changed = true;
 237 | |                   switch (ch) {
 238 | |                       case "\n":
 239 | |                           result += "\\n";
 240 | |                           break;
 241 | |                       case "\r":
 242 | |                           result += "\\r";
 243 | |                           break;
 244 | |                       case "\t":
 245 | |                           result += "\\t";
 246 | |                           break;
 247 | |                       case "\b":
 248 | |                           result += "\\b";
 249 | |                           break;
 250 | |                       case "\f":
 251 | |                           result += "\\f";
 252 | |                           break;
 253 | |                       default:
 254 | |                           result += `\\u${code.toString(16).padStart(4, "0")}`;
 255 | |                   }
 256 | |                   continue;
 257 | |               }
 258 | |               result += ch;
 259 | |               continue;
 260 | |           }
 261 | |           if (ch === '"') {
 262 | |               inString = true;
 263 | |           }
 264 | |           result += ch;
 265 | |       }
 266 | |       return changed ? result : value;
 267 | `-> }

  x eslint(complexity): function `tryParseJsonForTypes` has a complexity of 22. Maximum allowed is 12.
     ,-[packages/ai/src/utils/validation.ts:329:1]
 328 |      */
 329 | ,-> function tryParseJsonForTypes(value: string, expectedTypes: string[]): { value: unknown; changed: boolean } {
 330 | |       const trimmed = value.trim();
 331 | |       if (!trimmed) return { value, changed: false };
 332 | |   
 333 | |       const numberCoercion = tryParseNumberString(trimmed, expectedTypes);
 334 | |       if (numberCoercion.changed) {
 335 | |           return numberCoercion;
 336 | |       }
 337 | |   
 338 | |       // Quick syntactic checks to avoid unnecessary parse attempts
 339 | |       const looksJsonObject = trimmed.startsWith("{");
 340 | |       const looksJsonArray = trimmed.startsWith("[");
 341 | |       const looksJsonLiteral =
 342 | |           trimmed === "true" || trimmed === "false" || trimmed === "null" || JSON_NUMBER_PATTERN.test(trimmed);
 343 | |   
 344 | |       if (!looksJsonObject && !looksJsonArray && !looksJsonLiteral) {
 345 | |           return { value, changed: false };
 346 | |       }
 347 | |   
 348 | |       try {
 349 | |           const parsed = JSON.parse(trimmed) as unknown;
 350 | |           // If the string was "null", we parsed it to actual null.
 351 | |           // Accept this even if null isn't in expectedTypes - the LLM meant "no value".
 352 | |           // normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema will strip it from optional fields, and
 353 | |           // AJV will correctly error on required fields.
 354 | |           if (parsed === null && trimmed === "null") {
 355 | |               return { value: null, changed: true };
 356 | |           }
 357 | |           // For non-null values, only accept if the parsed type matches what the schema expects
 358 | |           if (matchesExpectedType(parsed, expectedTypes)) {
 359 | |               return { value: parsed, changed: true };
 360 | |           }
 361 | |       } catch {
 362 | |           if (looksJsonObject || looksJsonArray) {
 363 | |               // Try escaping raw control chars inside string literals (LLMs sometimes
 364 | |               // emit literal newlines/tabs inside string content rather than `\n`/`\t`).
 365 | |               const escapedControls = escapeRawControlsInJsonStrings(trimmed);
 366 | |               if (escapedControls !== trimmed) {
 367 | |                   try {
 368 | |                       const parsed = JSON.parse(escapedControls) as unknown;
 369 | |                       if (matchesExpectedType(parsed, expectedTypes)) {
 370 | |                           return { value: parsed, changed: true };
 371 | |                       }
 372 | |                   } catch {}
 373 | |               }
 374 | |               // Try extracting a valid JSON prefix (handles trailing junk after balanced container)
 375 | |               const leading = tryParseLeadingJsonContainer(trimmed);
 376 | |               if (leading !== undefined && matchesExpectedType(leading, expectedTypes)) {
 377 | |                   return { value: leading, changed: true };
 378 | |               }
 379 | |               // Try healing single-character bracket errors near the end of the string
 380 | |               const healed = tryHealMalformedJson(trimmed);
 381 | |               if (healed !== undefined && matchesExpectedType(healed, expectedTypes)) {
 382 | |                   return { value: healed, changed: true };
 383 | |               }
 384 | |           }
 385 | |           return { value, changed: false };
 386 | |       }
 387 | |   
 388 | |       return { value, changed: false };
 389 | `-> }

  x eslint(complexity): function `normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema` has a complexity of 44. Maximum allowed is 12.
     ,-[packages/ai/src/utils/validation.ts:473:1]
 472 |     
 473 | ,-> function normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema(schema: unknown, value: unknown): { value: unknown; changed: boolean } {
 474 | |       if (value === null || value === undefined) return { value, changed: false };
 475 | |       if (schema === null || typeof schema !== "object") return { value, changed: false };
 476 | |   
 477 | |       const schemaObject = schema as Record<string, unknown>;
 478 | |   
 479 | |       const normalizeAnyOfLike = (keyword: "anyOf" | "oneOf"): { value: unknown; changed: boolean } => {
 480 | |           const branches = schemaObject[keyword];
 481 | |           if (!Array.isArray(branches)) return { value, changed: false };
 482 | |   
 483 | |           let changedCandidate: { value: unknown; changed: true } | null = null;
 484 | |   
 485 | |           for (const branch of branches) {
 486 | |               const normalized = normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema(branch, value);
 487 | |               if (!normalized.changed) continue;
 488 | |   
 489 | |               try {
 490 | |                   const validateBranch = ajv.compile(branch);
 491 | |                   if (validateBranch(normalized.value)) {
 492 | |                       return normalized;
 493 | |                   }
 494 | |               } catch {
 495 | |                   // Ignore branch-level compilation/validation errors and keep scanning.
 496 | |               }
 497 | |   
 498 | |               if (!changedCandidate) {
 499 | |                   changedCandidate = { value: normalized.value, changed: true };
 500 | |               }
 501 | |           }
 502 | |   
 503 | |           return changedCandidate ?? { value, changed: false };
 504 | |       };
 505 | |   
 506 | |       const anyOfNormalization = normalizeAnyOfLike("anyOf");
 507 | |       if (anyOfNormalization.changed) return anyOfNormalization;
 508 | |   
 509 | |       const oneOfNormalization = normalizeAnyOfLike("oneOf");
 510 | |       if (oneOfNormalization.changed) return oneOfNormalization;
 511 | |   
 512 | |       if (Array.isArray(schemaObject.allOf)) {
 513 | |           let changed = false;
 514 | |           let nextValue: unknown = value;
 515 | |           for (const branch of schemaObject.allOf) {
 516 | |               const normalized = normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema(branch, nextValue);
 517 | |               if (!normalized.changed) continue;
 518 | |               nextValue = normalized.value;
 519 | |               changed = true;
 520 | |           }
 521 | |           if (changed) return { value: nextValue, changed: true };
 522 | |       }
 523 | |   
 524 | |       if (Array.isArray(value)) {
 525 | |           const itemSchema = schemaObject.items;
 526 | |           if (itemSchema === null || typeof itemSchema !== "object" || Array.isArray(itemSchema)) {
 527 | |               return { value, changed: false };
 528 | |           }
 529 | |   
 530 | |           let changed = false;
 531 | |           let nextValue = value;
 532 | |           for (let i = 0; i < value.length; i += 1) {
 533 | |               const normalized = normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema(itemSchema, value[i]);
 534 | |               if (!normalized.changed) continue;
 535 | |               if (!changed) {
 536 | |                   nextValue = [...value];
 537 | |                   changed = true;
 538 | |               }
 539 | |               nextValue[i] = normalized.value;
 540 | |           }
 541 | |           return { value: changed ? nextValue : value, changed };
 542 | |       }
 543 | |   
 544 | |       // Coerce string → number/integer when the schema branch declares those types.
 545 | |       // This fixes anyOf:[{type:"number"},{type:"null"}] (i.e. Optional<number>) where
 546 | |       // AJV reports an "anyOf" error rather than a "type" error, bypassing
 547 | |       // coerceArgsFromErrors which only handles keyword:"type" errors.
 548 | |       if ((schemaObject.type === "number" || schemaObject.type === "integer") && typeof value === "string") {
 549 | |           return tryParseNumberString(value, [schemaObject.type as string]);
 550 | |       }
 551 | |   
 552 | |       if (schemaObject.type !== "object") return { value, changed: false };
 553 | |       if (typeof value !== "object" || value === null) return { value, changed: false };
 554 | |       if (Array.isArray(value)) return { value, changed: false };
 555 | |       if (schemaObject.properties === null || typeof schemaObject.properties !== "object") {
 556 | |           return { value, changed: false };
 557 | |       }
 558 | |   
 559 | |       const properties = schemaObject.properties as Record<string, unknown>;
 560 | |       const required = new Set(Array.isArray(schemaObject.required) ? (schemaObject.required as string[]) : []);
 561 | |   
 562 | |       let changed = false;
 563 | |       let nextValue = value as Record<string, unknown>;
 564 | |   
 565 | |       for (const [key, propertySchema] of Object.entries(properties)) {
 566 | |           if (!(key in nextValue)) continue;
 567 | |           const currentValue = nextValue[key];
 568 | |   
 569 | |           // Strip null and the string "null" from optional fields.
 570 | |           // The LLM sometimes outputs string "null" to mean "no value".
 571 | |           if ((currentValue === null || currentValue === "null") && !required.has(key)) {
 572 | |               if (!changed) {
 573 | |                   nextValue = { ...nextValue };
 574 | |                   changed = true;
 575 | |               }
 576 | |               delete nextValue[key];
 577 | |               continue;
 578 | |           }
 579 | |           const normalized = normalizeOptionalNullsForSchema(propertySchema, currentValue);
 580 | |           if (!normalized.changed) continue;
 581 | |   
 582 | |           if (!changed) {
 583 | |               nextValue = { ...nextValue };
 584 | |               changed = true;
 585 | |           }
 586 | |           nextValue[key] = normalized.value;
 587 | |       }
 588 | |   
 589 | |       // Strip unknown keys with null/"null" values when the schema forbids extras.
 590 | |       // LLMs sometimes hallucinate verbs alongside valid ones (e.g. `split: null`,
 591 | |       // `original: null`). Rejecting the entire tool call wastes a turn; treating
 592 | |       // these the same as null on known optional fields is a safer fallback. Keys
 593 | |       // with non-null unknown values are left intact so genuine schema mistakes
 594 | |       // still surface as validation errors.
 595 | |       if (schemaObject.additionalProperties === false) {
 596 | |           const knownKeys = new Set(Object.keys(properties));
 597 | |           for (const key of Object.keys(nextValue)) {
 598 | |               if (knownKeys.has(key)) continue;
 599 | |               const v = nextValue[key];
 600 | |               if (v !== null && v !== "null") continue;
 601 | |               if (!changed) {
 602 | |                   nextValue = { ...nextValue };
 603 | |                   changed = true;
 604 | |               }
 605 | |               delete nextValue[key];
 606 | |           }
 607 | |       }
 608 | |   
 609 | |       return { value: changed ? nextValue : value, changed };
 610 | `-> }
